NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

residing at Old No. 5/23, New No. 3/680, Middle Street,
Vedalai Post, Ramanathapuram-623 804, has converted to
Islam with the name of SHARMILA on 3rd July 2008.
K. SASIKALA.
Ramanathapuram, 21st January 2011.

FORM No. 155
(See Rule 329)
Member’s Voluntary Winding Up
MGTS SOFTWARE PRIVATE LIMITED,
(In Liquidation),
Having Registered Office at Unit B-003,
Basement Omega-Wing, Raheja Towers,
New No. 177, Anna Salai,
Chennai-600 002.
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 that a General Meeting of the members of the above named company
will be held at Iyer & Thomas, 15/8, 7th Cross, Indira Nagar, Adyar, Chennai-600 020 on the 15th day of February 2011
at 11.00 a.m for the purpose of having an account laid before them showing the manner in which the winding-up has
been conducted and the property of the Company disposed of and of hearing any explanation that may be given by the
liquidator and also for determining by a special resolution of the Company the manner in which the books, accounts and
documents of the Company and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.
Dated this 3rd day of January 2011.
15/8, 7th Cross, Indira Nagar,
Adyar, Chennai-600 020.

H. KARTHIK SESHADRI,
Liquidator.
PUBLIC NOTICE

I, J. Karthikeyan, natural son of (Late) P.K. Jayaraman, residing at No. 9, West Vadampooki Street, Thirunageswaram
Post, Thanjavur District, Tamil Nadu. Pin-612 204, by way of this Public Notice, I inform, that (Late) Shri T.S. Kaliyaperumal
has legally adopted me as his son on 30th May 1984 by way a Registered Deed No. 16 of 1984, on the file of the
Sub-Registrar of Thiruvidaimarudur. My Adopted Father Shri. T.S. Kaliyaperumal passed away on 21st July 2007. Hereafter
I shall be known as K. KARTHIKEYAN.
Thirunageswaram,
14th January 2011.

J. KARTHIKEYAN.
